      <p style=\"opacity: 0; transform: matrix(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 30);\">Jibo experiences the world, and reacts with surprisingly thoughtful movements and responses that show he’s no ordinary bot. So while he’ll gladly snap a photo or send a message, he’ll also get to know you and the people you care about, for more meaningful relationships.</p>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n\n  </section></div>          <div class=\"entity entity-field-collection-item field-collection-item-field-section field--section--item loaded\">\n    <section class=\"block block-block block-block-8 block-learns-differently\">\n    <div class=\"content-wrapper\">\n    <div class=\"row\">\n      <div class=\"columns\">\n        <div class=\"content block-content\">\n                              <h2 class=\"block-title\"><span>He</span> <span>learns</span> <span>differently</span></h2>\n                              <p>Every experience teaches Jibo something new, like recognizing the faces and voices of close family and friends, charming kids with immersive bedtime stories, or MC’ing games for the family.
